hagia_sophia = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 151

	#date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 537.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 2

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = miaphysite
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = hagia_sophia_now_mosque
			}
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		}
		else = {
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = miaphysite
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = miaphysite
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_development_cost = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 1
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.01
			monthly_piety = 0.001
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 7000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.2
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_development_cost = 0.2
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
            global_missionary_strength = 0.002
			tolerance_own = 2
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.02
			monthly_piety = 0.002
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 960
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 14000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_culture_conversion_cost = -0.3
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.3
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		    local_missionary_maintenance_cost = -0.3
			local_development_cost = 0.3
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
            global_missionary_strength = 0.003
			tolerance_own = 3
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.03
			tolerance_heathen = 3
			monthly_piety = 0.003
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

stonehenge = {
	#province it starts in
	start = 7420

	#date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = -2500.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 2

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		    local_manpower_modifier = 0.10
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_hostile_movement_speed = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			leader_land_shock = 1
			hostile_attrition = 1
			shock_damage = 0.10
		}

		on_upgraded = {

	tier_2 = {

		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)

tower_of_london = {
	#province it starts in
	start = 236

	#date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1078.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 7

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1444
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture = normand
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = tower_of_london
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = tower_of_london
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture = normand

	}

		}

		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}

buddha_statues = {
	#province it starts in
	start = 2225

	#date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 570.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = buddha_small
		show_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_small
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {

		area_modifier = {
			local_friendly_movement_speed = 0.1

		country_modifiers = {

			yearly_karma_decay = 0.001
		}

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	starting_tier = 1

	type = monument

		culture = inca
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}

		show_ambient_object = machu_picchu

		culture = inca

			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture = inca
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

			months = 240

		}

		}

shwedagon_pagoda = {
	#province it starts in
	start = 4399

	#date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1362.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = shwedagon_pagoda
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = shwedagon_pagoda
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1775
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240

		hide_ambient_object = pyramid_of_cheops
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {

				culture = al_misr_arabic
				has_owner_culture = yes
				}

				culture = al_misr_arabic

		}

	starting_tier = 1

			shock_damage = 0.20
		}

				}

    date = 1124.01.01
    
    time = {
        months = 0
    }
    
    build_cost = 0
    
    can_be_moved = no
    
    move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
    
    starting_tier = 1
    
    type = monument

    build_trigger = {
        culture_group = british
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}		
    }

    on_built = {
    }
    
    on_destroyed = {
    }

    can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
	    culture_group = british
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}	
    }

    can_upgrade_trigger = {
        is_year = 1703
		culture_group = british
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}	
    }

    keep_trigger = {
    }

    tier_0 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 0
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 0
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
        }

        country_modifiers = {
        }

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }

    tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			army_tradition = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 7000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			army_tradition = 0.25
			prestige = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
	
	tier_3 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 960
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 14000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			army_tradition = 0.25
			prestige = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

    }

    starting_tier = 1
    
    type = monument

    build_trigger = {

		has_owner_religion = yes	
    }

    on_built = {
    }
    
    on_destroyed = {

    can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
        religion_group = christian
		has_owner_religion = yes		
    }

    can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1524
	    religion_group = christian
		has_owner_religion = yes
    }

    keep_trigger = {
    }

    tier_0 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 0
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 0
        }

        }

        area_modifier = {
        }

        country_modifiers = {
        }

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }

    tier_1 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 240
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 3500
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
		    local_unrest = 0.5
        }

        country_modifiers = {
		    church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
		    religious_unity = 0.05
			global_missionary_strength = 0.01
        }

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }
	
	tier_2 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 480
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 7000
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
		    local_unrest = 1
        }

        country_modifiers = {
		    church_loyalty_modifier = 0.15
		    religious_unity = 0.1
			global_missionary_strength = 0.02
			missionaries = 1
		}

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }
	
	tier_3 = {
        upgrade_time = {

		    local_unrest = 0.5 #independent thought = more unrest
        }

        country_modifiers = {
		    idea_cost = -0.0125 #free thinkers and the like would reduce idea cost
			advisor_cost = -0.0125 #more smart people = lower price for smart people
			innovativeness_gain = 0.125 #always been pretty forward thinking (might be OP stacked with Anglican but once you're capped you're capped!)
        }

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }
	
	tier_2 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 240
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 6000
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
		    local_unrest = 1
        }

        country_modifiers = {
		    idea_cost = -0.025 #free thinkers and the like would reduce idea cost
			advisor_cost = -0.025 #more smart people = lower price for smart people
			innovativeness_gain = 0.25 #always been pretty forward thinking (might be OP stacked with Anglican but once you're capped you're capped!)
		}

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }
	
	tier_3 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 480
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 8000
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
		    local_unrest = 1.5
        }

        country_modifiers = {
		    idea_cost = -0.05 #free thinkers and the like would reduce idea cost

palais_des_tuileries = { #Palais des Tuileries
	# province it starts in
	start = 183

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1563.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?

warsaw_castle = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 257		#Warsaw
	
	# date built in real life
	date = 1313.6.1
	
	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 24
	}
	
	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 500

	can_be_moved = no
	
	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	
	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 0	#Probably not significant enough in 1444 to start as tier 1

	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			is_capital = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
	
	}
	
	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
	
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			is_capital = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			FROM = { tag = MAZ }
			is_year = 1598		#Capital moved to Warsaw
		}
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			is_capital = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}	
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		province_modifiers = {
		}

		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.075
			local_defensiveness = 0.05
			local_unrest = -0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.05
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier

			local_tax_modifier = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier

		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.2
			local_build_cost = -0.2

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.075
			church_influence_modifier = 0.025

			warscore_cost_vs_other_religion = -0.05
			land_morale = 0.10
			tolerance_own = 1
			naval_forcelimit = 4
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			define_admiral = {
				shock = 3
				fire = 3
				manuever = 4
				siege = 2
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 7500
		}

			trade_value_modifier = 0.1
			trade_goods_size = 0.5
			trade_value = 2
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.1

			local_missionary_strength = -0.03
			local_regiment_cost = -0.2
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
			local_sailors_modifier = 0.25
			local_development_cost = -0.2
		}

		area_modifier = {

			local_unrest = -2

			province_trade_power_modifier = 0.1
			ship_recruit_speed = -0.1
		}

		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
			church_influence_modifier = 0.05
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.1
			warscore_cost_vs_other_religion = -0.10
			land_morale = 0.10
			missionaries = 1
			global_missionary_strength = 0.02
			tolerance_own = 1
			shock_damage_received = -0.025
			naval_forcelimit = 10
		}

		}

stora_kopparberget = { #Stora Kopparberget
    start = 8
    
    date = 1011.01.01             #Earliest records of it is in the 11th Century
    
    time = {
        months = 0
    }
    
    build_cost = 0
    
    can_be_moved = no
    
    move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
    
    starting_tier = 1
    
    type = monument

   build_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
				}
				tag = SWE
				tag = SCA
				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}
	}

    on_built = {
    }
    
    on_destroyed = {
    }

    can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
				}
				tag = SWE
				tag = SCA
				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}
	}

    can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1523		#Mining expansion subsidised by special taxes starts in early 1500
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
				}
				tag = SWE
				tag = SCA
				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}	
	}

    keep_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
